 ek adhikari ne kaha ki jiesti parishad ne pushti ke liye adhikariyon ko koi bhi anya prakaar kaa tarika adhishuchet karne kaa adhikaar diya he

 There are many beliefs about the Christmas tree
 aisa bhi mana jaataa he ki christmas tree ko ghar laane or sajaane se vaastu dosha dur hote hai
 1
 christmas par apane ghar main christmas tree jarur laaen or isaki acchhee tarah se sajaavat karen
 It is believed that decorating the Christmas tree gives luck and supports all kinds of negative energy from the house

 maine unase kaha tha ki aap kisi ko bhi upakptain chun sakate hai

 meri captain banane main koi ruchi nahin thi
 The World Cup game, which did not win due to Dhoni alone, was adamant on his 2012 statement in which he opposed giving credit for a World Cup win to a cricketer
 unhone chah july 2012 ko ek press conference main kaha tha ki team dhoni kii captaini kii vajah se world cap nahin jiti balki isliye jiti kyonki team ne acha pradarshan kiya tha
 Sehwag said, 'ask anyone present here whether my statement was true or false
 meraa bayaan galat nahin tha lekin use galat tareeke se pesh kiya gaya
 He said, 'I was not criticizing Dhoni
 maine itnaa hi kaha tha ki puraa shrey captain ko hi nahin balki team ko bhi diya janaa chahie
 Sehwag said, "if you look at the record, Dhoni is the best captain of India so far
 saurav ganguli ko pachhadkar unhone test, vanade or tii20 or do world cap jite
